name:l‚Äça‚Äçr‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçm‚Äça‚Äçn
info:Club Premium Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 19, 2024
msg:From Shanghai, we went on a parent-child hike to Meiwu Ancient Road. We didn't want to drive too long to downtown Shaoxing after getting off the mountain in the afternoon, so we chose the Marriott nearby. The hardware of the newly opened hotel last year is absolutely online, and the software service is also in place. The staff will take the initiative to greet the guests when they enter the door. Although the five-star training should be the same, many old Marriotts in Shanghai and other Jiangsu and Zhejiang rarely greet guests when they see them.
Executive Select is a little more expensive than ordinary executive, but the selected rooms are all corner rooms, with larger areas and 180-degree floor-to-ceiling windows, although there is no scenery outside. The executive lounge is simple biscuits and soft drinks in the afternoon, nothing special, but there is a freshly cooked noodle stall during the happy hour in the evening, which is not seen in other hotels. There are other ordinary basic fried rice and fried dishes. It is absolutely no problem to have a full meal in the lounge at night.
There is a seat for breakfast on the first floor, and all the food is available. The breakfast of the Marriott series tastes good.
The equipment in the gym is very complete, and the configuration of the new hotel is good.
The only disadvantage is the location, which is relatively remote. If you want to drive to the city, it will take another hour, but I didn't expect the occupancy rate to be low at all.
